High relevance threshold\n                            finding = {\n                                \'title\': title,\n                                \'link\': link,\n                                \'snippet\': snippet[:300],\n                                \'relevance_score\': relevance_score,\n                                \'indicators\': {k: v for k, v in relevance_indicators.items() if v},\n                                \'source\': \'serpapi\'\n                            }\n                            \n                            search_record[\'relevant_findings\'].append(finding)\n                            \n                            # Categorize findings\n                            if relevance_score >= 7 and relevance_indicators[\'1851\'] and relevance_indicators[\'chambers\']:\n                                print(f\'    ðŸ“š HIGH-PRIORITY BOOK CANDIDATE (Score: {relevance_score})\')\n                                search_results[\'book_candidates\'].append({\n                                    \'query\': query,\n                                    \'finding\': finding,\n                                    \'confidence\': \'very_high\' if relevance_score >= 9 else \'high\'\n                                })\n                            \n                            if relevance_indicators[\'2009\'] and relevance_indicators[\'reissued\']:\n                                print(f\'    ðŸ“… 2009 PUBLISHER CANDIDATE (Score: {relevance_score})\')\n                                search_results[\'publisher_candidates\'].append({\n                                    \'query\': query,\n                                    \'finding\': finding\n                                })\n                            \n                            print(f\'    âœ“ Relevant result (Score: {relevance_score}): {title[:80]}...\')\n                    \n                    search_record[\'success\'] = len(search_record[\'relevant_findings\']) > 0\n                    \n                else:\n                    print(\'  âš  No SERPAPI organic results\')\n            else:\n                print(f\'  âœ— SERPAPI failed: HTTP {response.status_code}\')\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\'  âœ— SERPAPI error: {str(e)}\')\n    \n    # Method 2: Direct web search fallback\n    if not search_record[\'success\']:\n        try:\n            print(\'  â†’ Using direct web search...\')\n            \n            headers = {\n                \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n                \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8\',\n                \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.5\'\n            }\n            \n            # Encode query for Google search\n            encoded_query = quote_plus(query)\n            search_url = f\'https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num=10\'\n            \n            response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=25)\n            \n            if response.status_code == 200:\n                content = response.text.lower()\n                \n                # Check for key terms\n                key_terms = [\'1851\', \'chambers\', \'phrenology\', \'mesmerism\', \'atheistic\', \'naturalism\', \'2009\', \'controversial\', \'vestiges\']\n                found_terms = [term for term in key_terms if term in content]\n                \n                if len(found_terms) >= 4:  # Minimum relevance for direct search\n                    search_record[\'method_used\'] = \'direct_web\'\n                    search_record[\'results_found\'] = 1\n                    \n                    # Extract page title\n                    title_match = re.search(r\'<title[^>]*>([^<]+)</title>\', response.text, re.IGNORECASE)\n                    page_title = title_match.group(1).strip() if title_match else \'Google Search Results\'\n                    \n                    finding = {\n                        \'title\': page_title,\n                        \'found_terms\': found_terms,\n                        \'relevance_score\': len(found_terms),\n                        \'source\': \'direct_web\',\n                        \'url\': search_url\n                    }\n                    \n                    search_record[\'relevant_findings\'].append(finding)\n                    search_record[\'success\'] = True\n                    \n                    print(f\'  âœ“ Direct search success - found {len(found_terms)} terms: {',
    ".join(found_terms)}')
                    
                    # High-value direct results
                    if len(found_terms) >= 6:
                        search_results['key_findings'].append({
                            'query': query,
                            'finding': finding,
                            'type': 'high_value_direct_result'
                        })
                        print(f'    ðŸŽ¯ HIGH-VALUE DIRECT RESULT')
                else:
                    print(f'  âš  Direct search: only {len(found_terms)} relevant terms found')
            else:
                print(f'  âœ— Direct search failed: HTTP {response.status_code}')
                
        except Exception as e:
            print(f'  âœ— Direct search error: {str(e)}')
    
    if not search_record['success']:
        print('  âŒ No relevant results found')
    
    return search_record

# Execute all comprehensive searches
print('=== EXECUTING COMPREHENSIVE SEARCHES ===')
print('=' * 70)

for i, query in enumerate(comprehensive_queries, 1):
    print(f'\n[{i}/{len(comprehensive_queries)}]')
    
    search_record = execute_comprehensive_search(query, i)
    search_results['searches_conducted'].append(search_record)
    
    # Rate limiting
    time.sleep(2.5)

# Comprehensive analysis of all results

quote_plus\n    \n    search_record = {\n        \'index\': search_index,\n        \'query\': query,\n        \'timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%H:%M:%S\'),\n        \'success\': False,\n        \'results_found\': 0,\n        \'relevant_findings\': [],\n        \'error\': None\n    }\n    \n    print(f\'Search {search_index}: {query}\')\n    \n    try:\n        # Proper headers for Google        encoded_query = quote_plus(query)\n        search_url = f\'https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num=20&hl=en\'\n        \n        print(\'  â†’ Executing search request...\')\n book_patterns = [\n                r\'robert chambers.*?1851.*?(?:book|work|publication)\',\n                r\'william chambers.*?1851.*?(?:book|work|publication)\',\n                r\'chambers.*?1851.*?(?:phrenology|mesmerism)\',\n                r\'1851.*?chambers.*?(?:atheistic|naturalism)\',\n                r\'vestiges.*?sequel.*?1851\',\n                r\'explanations.*?chambers.*?1851\',\n                r\'natural history.*?creation.*?1851\'\n            ]\n            \n            # Define patterns for 2009 reissues\n            reissue_patterns = [\n                r\'(?:reissued|republished|reprinted).*?2009\',\n                r\'2009.*?(?:edition|reprint|publication)\',\n                r\'cambridge.*?press.*?2009\',\n                r\'oxford.*?press.*?2009\',\n                r\'harvard.*?press.*?2009\'\n            ]\n            \n            # Analyze content for book references\n            book_references = []\n            for pattern in book_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, page_content, re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL)\n                if matches:\n Filter to only terms that were found\n            found_terms = {k: v for k, v in key_terms.items() if v > 0}\n            search_record[\'content_found\'] = found_terms\n            \n            # Calculate relevance score\n            relevance_score = 0\n            for term, count in found_terms.items():\n                # Weight certain terms more heavily\n                if term in [\'1851\', \'chambers\', \'phrenology\', \'mesmerism\']:\n                    relevance_score += min(count, 5) * 2  # Cap at 5 occurrences, weight x2\n                elif term in [\'atheistic\', \'naturalism\', \'vestiges\', \'explanations\']:\n                    relevance_score += min(count, 3) * 1.5  # Cap at 3, weight x1.5\n                else:\n                    relevance_score += min(count, 2)  # Cap at 2 occurrences\n            \n            search_record[\'relevance_score\'] = int(relevance_score)\n            \n            print(f\'  âœ“ Found terms: {list(found_terms.keys())}\')\n            print(f\'  âœ“ Relevance score: {search_record["relevance_score"]}\')\n            \n            # Look for book-related patterns\n            book_patterns = [\n                \'robert chambers.*1851\',\n                \'william chambers.*1851\', \n                \'1851.*chambers.*phrenology\',\n                \'1851.*chambers.*mesmerism\',\n                \'vestiges.*sequel.*1851\',\n                \'explanations.*chambers.*1851\',\n                \'chambers.*1851.*atheistic\',\n                \'chambers.*1851.*naturalism\'\n            ]\n            \n            book_indicators = []\n            for pattern in book_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, page_content, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if matches:\n                    book_indicators.extend(matches[:2])  # Limit to 2 matches per pattern\n            \n            search_record[\'book_indicators\'] = book_indicators[:5]  # Top 5 indicators\n            \n            # Look for publisher patterns\n            publisher_patterns = [\n                \'2009.*edition\',\n                \'2009.*reprint\',\n                \'reissued.*2009\',\n                \'republished.*2009\',\n                \'cambridge.*press.*2009\',\n                \'oxford.*press.*2009\',\n                \'harvard.*press.*2009\'\n            ]\n            \n            publisher_indicators = []\n            for pattern in publisher_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, page_content, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if matches:\n                    publisher_indicators.extend(matches[:2])\n            \n            search_record[\'publisher_indicators\'] = publisher_indicators[:3]  # Top 3\n            \n            # Determine if this is a successful search\n            if search_record[\'relevance_score\'] >= 10:\n                search_record[\'success\'] = True\n                print(\'  ðŸŽ¯ HIGH-RELEVANCE CONTENT FOUND!\')\n                \n                # Check if this qualifies as a book candidate\n                if (found_terms.get(\'1851\', 0) > 0 and \n                    found_terms.get(\'chambers\', 0) > 0 and \n                    (found_terms.get(\'phrenology\', 0) > 0 or found_terms.get(\'mesmerism\', 0) > 0)):\n                    \n                    book_candidate = {\n                        \'query\': query,\n                        \'relevance_score\': search_record[\'relevance_score\'],\n                        \'found_terms\': found_terms,\n                        \'book_indicators\': book_indicators,\n                        \'confidence\': \'high\' if search_record[\'relevance_score\'] >= 20 else \'medium\'\n                    }\n                    \n                    search_results[\'book_candidates\'].append(book_candidate)\n                    print(\'    ðŸ“š BOOK CANDIDATE IDENTIFIED!\')\n                \n                # Check if this qualifies as a publisher candidate\n                if found_terms.get(\'2009\', 0) > 0 and publisher_indicators:\n                    publisher_candidate = {\n                        \'query\': query,\n                        \'publisher_indicators\': publisher_indicators,\n                        \'found_terms\': found_terms\n                    }\n                    \n                    search_results[\'publisher_candidates\'].append(publisher_candidate)\n                    print(\'    ðŸ“… PUBLISHER CANDIDATE IDENTIFIED!\')\n                    \n            elif search_record[\'relevance_score\'] >= 5:\n                search_record[\'success\'] = True\n                print(\'  âœ“ Medium relevance content found\')\n            \n            # Add to content analysis\n            search_results[\'content_analysis\'].append({\n                \'query\': query,\n                \'relevance_score\': search_record[\'relevance_score\'],\n                \'found_terms\': found_terms,\n                \'book_indicators_count\': len(book_indicators),\n                \'publisher_indicators_count\': len(publisher_indicators)\n            })\n            \n        else:\n            print(f\'  âœ— HTTP request failed: {response.status_code}\')\n            search_record[\'error\'] = f\'HTTP {response.status_code}\'\n            \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  âœ— Search error: {str(e)}\')\n        search_record[\'error\'] = str(e)\n    \n    if not search_record[\'success\']:\n        print(\'  âŒ No significant content found\')\n    \n    return search_record\n\n# Execute all comprehensive searches\nprint(\'=== EXECUTING COMPREHENSIVE WEB SEARCHES ===\')\nprint(\'=\' * 70)\n\nfor i, query in enumerate(comprehensive_queries, 1):\n    print(f\'\\n[{i}/{len(comprehensive_queries)}]\')\n    \n    search_record = execute_comprehensive_search(query, i)\n    search_results[\'searches_conducted\'].append(search_record)\n    \n    # Rate limiting to avoid being blocked\n    time.sleep(4)\n\n# Comprehensive analysis of results\nprint(\'\\n\\n\' + \'=\' * 80)\nprint(\'COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS OF SEARCH RESULTS\')\nprint(\'=\' * 80)\n\n# Calculate statistics\ntotal_searches = len(search_results[\'searches_conducted\'])\nsuccessful_searches = len([s for s in search_results[\'searches_conducted\'] if s[\'success\']])\nbook_candidates = len(search_results[\'book_candidates\'])\npublisher_candidates = len(search_results[\'publisher_candidates\'])\ntotal_relevance = sum(s[\'relevance_score\'] for s in search_results[\'searches_conducted\'])\n\nprint(f\'\\nðŸ“Š SEARCH STATISTICS:\')\nprint(f\'  Total searches conducted: {total_searches}\')\nprint(f\'  Successful searches: {successful_searches}\')\nprint(f\'  Success rate: {100*successful_searches/total_searches:.1f}%\')\nprint(f\'  Total relevance score: {total_relevance}\')\nprint(f\'  Average relevance per search: {total_relevance/total_searches:.1f}\')\nprint(f\'  Book identification candidates: {book_candidates}\')\nprint(f\'  Publisher identification candidates: {publisher_candidates}\')\n\n# Display book candidates\nif search_results[\'book_candidates\']:\n    print(\'\\nðŸ“š BOOK IDENTIFICATION CANDIDATES:\')\n    print(\'-\' * 70)\n    \n    #     "code": 'import os\nimport requests\nimport time\nimport json\nimport re\n\nprint(\'=== FINAL COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR 1851 ATHEISTIC NATURALISM BOOK ===\')\nprint(\'Target: Co-authored 1851 book advocating atheistic naturalism with phrenology/mesmerism\')\nprint(\'Objective: Identify specific book title, authors, and 2009 reissue publisher\\n\')\n\n# Ensure workspace directory exists\nos.makedirs(\'workspace\', exist_ok=True)\n\n# First, let\'s check if we have previous search results to analyze\nprevious_results_file = \'workspace/comprehensive_1851_book_search_results.json\'\n\nif os.path.exists(previous_results_file):\n    print(\'Found previous search results file. Inspecting structure first...\')\n    \n    with open(previous_results_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        previous_data = json.load(f)\n    \n    print(\'Previous results file structure:\')\n    print(f\'Keys: {list(previous_data.keys())}\')\n    if \'searches_conducted\' in previous_data:\n        print(f\'Total searches: {len(previous_data["searches_conducted"])}\')\n    if \'content_analysis\' in previous_data:\n        print(f\'Content analysis entries: {len(previous_data["content_analysis"])}\')\n    print(\'\\n\')\n\n# Initialize global search results structure\nglobal_search_results = {\n    \'search_timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\'),\n    \'objective\': \'Identify 1851 co-authored atheistic naturalism book with phrenology/mesmerism and 2009 reissue\',\n    \'method\': \'fixed_scope_comprehensive_search\',\n    \'searches_conducted\': [],\n    \'book_candidates\': [],\n    \'publisher_candidates\': [],\n    \'key_findings\': [],\n    \'content_analysis\': []\n}\n\n# Define targeted search queries based on HISTORY success patterns\ntargeted_queries = [\n    # High-scoring queries from HISTORY\n    \'1851 phrenology mesmerism book "reissued 2009" "republished 2009"\',  # Score 36 in HISTORY\n    \'"Vestiges" Chambers 1851 sequel phrenology mesmerism naturalism\',     # Score 11 in HISTORY\n    \'"Explanations" Chambers 1851 phrenology mesmerism co-authored\',       # Score 10 in HISTORY\n    \'"1851" "phrenology" "mesmerism" "atheistic naturalism" "co-authored"\', # Score 10 in HISTORY\n    \n    # Additional strategic searches\n    \'Robert Chambers William Chambers 1851 Edinburgh co-authored atheistic\',\n    \'"Explanations: A Sequel to Vestiges" 1851 phrenology mesmerism\',\n    \'Chambers brothers 1851 phrenology mesmerism controversial naturalism\',\n    \'Victorian 1851 phrenology mesmerism atheistic "Cambridge Press 2009"\',\n    \'1851 Edinburgh Chambers phrenology mesmerism "Oxford Press 2009"\',\n    \'Robert Chambers 1851 atheistic naturalism "Harvard Press 2009"\'\n]\n\nprint(f\'Prepared {len(targeted_queries)} targeted search queries based on HISTORY success patterns\\n\')\n\ndef execute_fixed_scope_search(query, search_index, results_container):\n    """Execute search with fixed variable scoping"""\n    \n    # Import within function to avoid scoping issues\n    from urllib.parse import quote_plus\n    \n    search_record = {\n        \'index\': search_index,\n        \'query\': query,\n        \'timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%H:%M:%S\'),\n        \'success\': False,\n        \'content_found\': {},\n        \'book_indicators\': [],\n        \'publisher_indicators\': [],\n        \'relevance_score\': 0,\n        \'error\': None\n    }\n    \n    print(f\'Search {search_index}: {query}\')\n    \n    try:\n        # Setup request headers\n        headers = {\n            \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n            \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8\',\n            \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.5\',\n            \'Connection\': \'keep-alive\'\n        }\n        \n        # Encode query and make request\n        encoded_query = quote_plus(query)\n        search_url = f\'https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num=20&hl=en\'\n        \n        print(\'  â†’ Executing search request...\')\n        response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            print(f\'  âœ“ HTTP {response.status_code} - analyzing content...\')\n            \n            # Convert to lowercase for analysis\n            page_content = response.text.lower()\n            \n            # Define key terms to search for\n            key_terms = {\n                \'1851\': 0,\n                \'chambers\': 0,\n                \'robert chambers\': 0,\n                \'william chambers\': 0,\n                \'phrenology\': 0,\n                \'mesmerism\': 0,\n                \'atheistic\': 0,\n                \'naturalism\': 0,\n                \'vestiges\': 0,\n                \'explanations\': 0,\n                \'controversial\': 0,\n                \'co-authored\': 0,\n                \'edinburgh\': 0,\n                \'2009\': 0,\n                \'reissued\': 0,\n                \'republished\': 0,\n                \'cambridge press\': 0,\n                \'oxford press\': 0,\n                \'harvard press\': 0\n            }\n            \n            # Count occurrences of each term\n            for term in key_terms:\n                count = page_content.count(term)\n                if count > 0:\n                    key_terms[term] = count\n            \n            # Filter to only terms that were found\n            found_terms = {k: v for k, v in key_terms.items() if v > 0}\n            search_record[\'content_found\'] = found_terms\n            \n            # Calculate relevance score with weighted terms\n            relevance_score = 0\n            for term, count in found_terms.items():\n                # Weight certain terms more heavily\n                if term in [\'1851\', \'chambers\', \'phrenology\', \'mesmerism\']:\n                    relevance_score += min(count, 5) * 2  # Cap at 5 occurrences, weight x2\n                elif term in [\'atheistic\', \'naturalism\', \'vestiges\', \'explanations\']:\n                    relevance_score += min(count, 3) * 1.5  # Cap at 3, weight x1.5\n                elif term in [\'2009\', \'reissued\', \'republished\']:\n                    relevance_score += min(count, 3) * 1.5  # Weight reissue terms\n                else:\n                    relevance_score += min(count, 2)  # Cap at 2 occurrences\n            \n            search_record[\'relevance_score\'] = int(relevance_score)\n            \n            print(f\'  âœ“ Found terms: {list(found_terms.keys())}\')\n            print(f\'  âœ“ Relevance score: {search_record["relevance_score"]}\')\n            \n            # Look for book-related patterns\n            book_patterns = [\n                r\'robert chambers.*1851\',\n                r\'william chambers.*1851\', \n                r\'1851.*chambers.*phrenology\',\n                r\'1851.*chambers.*mesmerism\',\n                r\'vestiges.*sequel.*1851\',\n                r\'explanations.*chambers.*1851\',\n                r\'chambers.*1851.*atheistic\',\n                r\'chambers.*1851.*naturalism\'\n            ]\n            \n            book_indicators = []\n            for pattern in book_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, page_content, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if matches:\n                    book_indicators.extend(matches[:2])  # Limit to 2 matches per pattern\n            \n            search_record[\'book_indicators\'] = book_indicators[:5]  # Top 5 indicators\n            \n            # Look for publisher patterns\n            publisher_patterns = [\n                r\'2009.*edition\',\n                r\'2009.*reprint\',\n                r\'reissued.*2009\',\n                r\'republished.*2009\',\n                r\'cambridge.*press.*2009\',\n                r\'oxford.*press.*2009\',\n                r\'harvard.*press.*2009\'\n            ]\n            \n            publisher_indicators = []\n            for pattern in publisher_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, page_content, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if matches:\n                    publisher_indicators.extend(matches[:2])\n            \n            search_record[\'publisher_indicators\'] = publisher_indicators[:3]  # Top 3\n            \n            # Determine if this is a successful search\n            if search_record[\'relevance_score\'] >= 10:\n                search_record[\'success\'] = True\n                print(\'  ðŸŽ¯ HIGH-RELEVANCE CONTENT FOUND!\')\n                \n                # Check if this qualifies as a book candidate\n                if (found_terms.get(\'1851\', 0) > 0 and \n                    found_terms.get(\'chambers\', 0) > 0 and \n                    (found_terms.get(\'phrenology\', 0) > 0 or found_terms.get(\'mesmerism\', 0) > 0)):\n                    \n                    book_candidate = {\n                        \'query\': query,\n                        \'relevance_score\': search_record[\'relevance_score\'],\n                        \'found_terms\': found_terms,\n                        \'book_indicators\': book_indicators,\n                        \'confidence\': \'very_high\' if search_record[\'relevance_score\'] >= 30 else \'high\' if search_record[\'relevance_score\'] >= 20 else \'medium\'\n                    }\n                    \n                    results_container[\'book_candidates\'].append(book_candidate)\n                    print(\'    ðŸ“š BOOK CANDIDATE IDENTIFIED!\')\n                \n                # Check if this qualifies as a publisher candidate\n                if found_terms.get(\'2009\', 0) > 0 and publisher_indicators:\n                    publisher_candidate = {\n                        \'query\': query,\n                        \'publisher_indicators\': publisher_indicators,\n                        \'found_terms\': found_terms,\n                        \'relevance_score\': search_record[\'relevance_score\']\n                    }\n                    \n                    results_container[\'publisher_candidates\'].append(publisher_candidate)\n                    print(\'    ðŸ“… PUBLISHER CANDIDATE IDENTIFIED!\')\n                    \n            elif search_record[\'relevance_score\'] >= 5:\n                search_record[\'success\'] = True\n                print(\'  âœ“ Medium relevance content found\')\n            \n            # Add to content analysis\n            results_container[\'content_analysis\'].append({\n                \'query\': query,\n                \'relevance_score\': search_record[\'relevance_score\'],\n                \'found_terms\': found_terms,\n                \'book_indicators_count\': len(book_indicators),\n                \'publisher_indicators_count\': len(publisher_indicators)\n            })\n            \n        else:\n            print(f\'  âœ— HTTP request failed: {response.status_code}\')\n            search_record[\'error\'] = f\'HTTP {response.status_code}\'\n            \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  âœ— Search error: {str(e)}\')\n        search_record[\'error\'] = str(e)\n    \n    if not search_record[\'success\']:\n        print(\'  âŒ No significant content found\')\n    \n    return search_record\n\n# Execute all targeted searches\nprint(\'=== EXECUTING TARGETED WEB SEARCHES WITH FIXED SCOPING ===\')\nprint(\'=\' * 70)\n\nfor i, query in enumerate(targeted_queries, 1):\n    print(f\'\\n[{i}/{len(targeted_queries)}]\')\n    \n    search_record = execute_fixed_scope_search(query, i, global_search_results)\n    global_search_results[\'searches_conducted\'].append(search_record)\n    \n    # Rate limiting to avoid being blocked\n    time.sleep(4)\n\n# Comprehensive analysis of results\nprint(\'\\n\\n\' + \'=\' * 80)\nprint(\'COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS OF SEARCH RESULTS\')\nprint(\'=\' * 80)\n\n# Calculate statistics\ntotal_searches = len(global_search_results[\'searches_conducted\'])\nsuccessful_searches = len([s for s in global_search_results[\'searches_conducted\'] if s[\'success\']])\nbook_candidates = len(global_search_results[\'book_candidates\'])\npublisher_candidates = len(global_search_results[\'publisher_candidates\'])\ntotal_relevance = sum(s[\'relevance_score\'] for s in global_search_results[\'searches_conducted\'])\n\nprint(f\'\\nðŸ“Š SEARCH STATISTICS:\')\nprint(f\'  Total searches conducted: {total_searches}\')\nprint(f\'  Successful searches: {successful_searches}\')\nprint(f\'  Success rate: {100*successful_searches/total_searches:.1f}%\')\nprint(f\'  Total relevance score: {total_relevance}\')\nprint(f\'  Average relevance per search: {total_relevance/total_searches:.1f}\')\nprint(f\'  Book identification candidates: {book_candidates}\')\nprint(f\'  Publisher identification candidates: {publisher_candidates}\')\n\n# Display book candidates\nif global_search_results[\'book_candidates\']:\n    print(\'\\nðŸ“š BOOK IDENTIFICATION CANDIDATES:\')\n    print(\'-\' * 70)\n    \n    #
